<H>{@sāraḷā mahābhārata
<>droṇaparba
<>duyyodhanara mḷeccharājā sahita bheṭa
<>o jaḷadhara byuha darśana@}
<P>jaẏatu lokeśwara nātha abhaẏe bāluṃkā
<P>saṃsāra nāśāṃgatā tuhi se siddha ẏekā | 1 |
<P>śuddha saṣṭika nirākuḷa nirastaka
<P>niśākara mauḷi nātha jaẏatu triẏambaka | 2 |
<P>agāda saṃsāra sāgara aṭai ẏe māẏā
<P>samasta goṣṭhī kalu nātha hoi ẏeka kāẏā | 3 |
<P>bhogeṇa bhoga swāmī rogeṇa pramāda
<P>samasta upekṣi cintilu paramapada | 4 |
<P>nirākāra puruṣa nikaḷaṃka kāẏāgoṭi
<P>anīti saṃsāru mote uddhara dhr̥jaṭī | 5 |
<P1>2| śuddha saṣṭika nirākuḷa nīḷakaṇu nikaḷaṃka candra
<>niśākara mauḷi deba jaẏatu kāśīrudra | (ṭa)
<P1>4|1 bhogeṇa bhogī swāmī bhābeṇa apramāda | (adhikāṃśa pothi)
[MBO-08-2]
<P>kāmyeka puruṣa nātha kāminī arddhakāẏā
<P>kāma niśodhana nātha aboṅgtra sadaẏā | 6 |
<P>naẏana pañchadaśa swabhābe kuṇḍaḷī
<P>girijāra saṅge ye sāmaratha triśūḷī | 7 |
<P>sajjana janara tu hr̥dagate japāmāḷi
<P>bhairoba mūrati dhari chāpilu mahābaḷī | 8 |
<P>śrībhmaje paśupatra khaṭwāṅga ye śara
<P>śireṇa dhabaḷī ye pinākī dhanurddhara | 9 |
<P>tripura ḍhaṃsilu nātha kautuka kheḷe
<P>andheka bināśilu bāḷalīḷā beḷe | 10 |
<P>yogeṇa yogeśwara swāmī samare jagujitā
<P>catrabhedī bāraṇa nātha parama pada śakatā | 11 |
<P>saṃsāra tāraṇa nātha kāḷakūṭa bhakṣi
<P>āpaṇā sukhe bhikṣāśī saẏaḷa janarakṣī | 12 |
<P>namo namo deba nīḷakaṇṭha nirālamba śwetarūpī
<P>yābata candrārke nātha tohora kāẏā byāpi | 13 |
<P>ghora antaka tāraṇa yāhāra nāmagoṭi
<P>muhiṃ talaẏe karai dibārātre heṭi | 14 |
<P>yoge yogeśwara swāmī gyāna upagata
<P>sādhanā siddha swāmī abhaẏe biśwanātha | 15 |
<P>patnīra nidhane kope dakṣayagyaṃ bhañjā
<P>mahā brahmahatyā doṣa bahane yugagañjā | 16 |
<P>surasiddha muni yāhāra caraṇa bande
<P>muhiṃ tāhā bhajilaiṃ parama sānande | 17 |
<P1>15|2 yāhāra udaru jāta sakaḷa jagata | (ña)
<P1>16|2 mahāpuruṣa nātha sakaḷa pāpabhāra gañjā | (ba, ga)
<P1>10|1 ḍhaṃsilu--dhwaṃsilu |
[MBO-08-3]
<P>saindu bāma ghora tatapurukha īśāna
<P>nandī mahākāḷa tule kāpāḷī bidyamāna | 18 |
<P>somapāḷa mantre saẏaḷa jana tārantā
<P>iha paralokakaiṃ pāḷana karantā | 19 |
<P>jaẏatu jagabandhu prabhma digāmbara
<P>ẏe bhaba bārādhi madhyuṃ bāreka uddhara | 20 |
<P>praḷaẏa uddhāraṇa nātha arddhāṅga bhabānī
<P>śūdramuni sāroḷa dāsara ghenimā daẏinī | 21 |
<P>he budhajane mohora na ghenimā doṣa
<P>janmeṇa abhyāsa nahiṃ karicchi sāhasa | 22 |
<P>mūrkha apaṇḍita muṃ najāṇai kicchi
<P>kiñchite sudaẏā mote kaleka piṅgaḷācchī | 23 |
<P>ādi anta madhye yāra abasāna nāhiṃ
<P>paramagati icchili tāhāra caraṇa dāhi | 24 |
<P>namaste jaṅkhera purabāsī tumbhe kara rakṣā
<P>āpaṇe dukhabhāgī saẏaḷa jana sākhā | 25 |
<P>śrīcaṇḍī sāroḷā caraṇe śaraṇa
<P>śūdramuni sāraḷā dāsaku karibu debī kāraṇa | 26 |
<P>baibasuta manu pucchākale śuṇimā agastiẏe
<P>tumbhe prasanne muṃlabhili saṃdehe | 27 |
<P>baibasuta manu pucchākale bhīṣmapaboṅg antareṇa kathā
<P>icchudaṇḍara madhye aṣṭādaśa paboṅgra bāratā | 28 |
<P1>19|1 sarbaloka bandhu haratā karantā |(ca, jha)
<P1>20|2 bhaba bārādhi nimagne nātha sacintya saẏaḷa |(ca, jha)
<P1>21|1 saẏaḷa jana tāraṇa caubarga dānī |(bahupothi)
<P1>22|2 ẏe janme na paḍhili gata janmara abhyāsa |(ga, ca)
<P1>23|2 piṅgaḷāccthī-piṅgaḷākṣī |
<P1>24|2 dāhi-dhyāẏi |
[MBO-08-4]
<P>bho deba kehu kaḷipāriba gaṅgābāli kari lekhā
<P>baḍabānaḷa bhitare ke deba kāṭhiyokhā | 29 |
<P>kr̥pājaḷa nandinī prasanne heṅguḷā
<P>hr̥dagate sumarai muhiṃ śrīṇḍī sāroḷā | 30 |
<P>maruḷa āsane māgo jaṅkherapura bāsī
<P>bhabitabya duṣukr̥ta karantā udāsī | 31 |
<P>aneka yugara pāpa hoilāka ḍhaṃsi
<P>yāhāra nāma dharante yamadaṇḍa nāśi | 32 |
<P>haraṇī tāraṇī go śrī sāroḷā debī caṇḍī
<P>taba kr̥pā hoile go kahibi droṇapaboṅg kāṇṭi | 33 |
<P>mahābhāratha bhīṣmapaboṅg daśadina antare
<P>muhiṃ tāhā bhābi cintili mama bakṣasthaḷe | 34 |
<P>narmadā saraswatī caraṇe mora sebā
<P>śūdramuni sāroḷa dāsaku mukati bāṭa debā | 35 |
<P>baibasuta manu pucchākale agastiṃki
<P>mānagobinda galā ye bhīṣmaṃkara tahiṃki | 36 |
<P>aneka bāge ye tiārile gāṅgabe
<P>se bacana upekṣiṇa kemanta kale kurudebe | 37 |
<P>śuṇa baibasuta manu badaẏanti brahmachārī
<P>baila harāi yehne loḍai kr̥ṣikārī | 38 |
<P>pantha na pāi yehne loḍai andhaḷi
<P>bhīṣmaṃkara abhābe rājāra citta antarāḷi | 39 |
<P>digāmbarī hoi rājā bhramai kurupati
<P>aruṇa prakāśe dekhilā droṇa senāpati | 40 |
<P>droṇa moile bābu bātuḷi kisa arthe
<P>mānagobinde boilā guru he bhīṣma ẏemanta kale mote | 41 |
<P1>32|1 jaẏatu siṃghabāhinī jhaṅkherapura bāsī | (cha, jha, ṭa)
<P1>38|2 baila = baḷada |
[MBO-08-5]
<P>droṇe boile āmbhe tote sandeśa kahibuṃ
<P>antapure bijekara tumbhe, āmbhe nityakarma sāribuṃ | 42 |
<P>karmaku santāpi rājā caḷai mānacatrabratī
<P>nairuta parbate yāiṃ bijaẏe pāhānti | 43 |
<P>meḷaccha deśara maẏa nāme asura rājā
<P>baḍāi kāmarūpī se aṭai danujā | 44 |
<P>batiśa marbhmata tule aneka mukuṭabandhā yodhī
<P>tāhāra gabanteṇa kampai bārānidhi | 45 |
<P>ḍagara mukhuṃ rājā mahābhāratha yuddha śuṇi
<P>sambhare āsai se thāṭha ye palāṇi | 46 |
<P>nairuta parbate se bijaẏe dhr̥tirāṣṭi
<P>yānteṇa meḷacchabaḷa sannidhye yāiṃ bheṭi | 47 |
<P>adabhmate thāṭha dekhi pachārai kurupati
<P>pañchāḷa saini prāẏe bujhi rājā manare kalā bhīti | 48 |
<P>āsanteṇa yoddhāẏe ye karanti pahija
<P>kurupāṇḍabe yebaṇa baḷa ocha tāku debā aiśuryya | 49 |
<P>anāsta lokakaiṃ ye karanti kāraṇa
<P>chatrīkuḷaku jāṇimānā sehi se baḍajaṇa | 50 |
<P>ẏesaneka śuṇi rājā manare sānande
<P>thāṭha sannidhye bije rājā mānagobinde | 51 |
<P>bābhiẏe kebaṇa deśara tumbhe aṭa mahīpāḷa
<P>rājyadhara mūrati dekhiṇa ye rahile sarbabaḷa | 52 |
<P>yoddhāẏe boile tumbhe kebaṇa deśara nr̥pati
<P>rājyadhara prāẏeka ta diśai tora mr̥tti | 53 |
<P>mānagobinda boilā muṃ kuñjagaḷa deśa adhikārī
<P>muhiṃ se pāṇḍabaṃkara tule bibāde bairi | 54 |
<P1>45|2 tāhāra laṃghante kampai bārānidhi |(cha, jha, ṭa)
[MBO-08-6]
<P>bhīṣma bolikari yebaṇa mahārathī
<P>tāhāṃkara pratagyāṃẏe muṃ pāṇḍabe hoili aprīti | 55 |
<P>icchāmr̥tu bānā tāhāra nija karma
<P>praśurāma chāribhāinta se jiṇile sāṃgrāma | 56 |
<P>bipāka karma mohora ye daiba abaḷe
<P>se hāde śaraśayyā kale yuddhakāḷe | 57 |
<P>tāhāṃkara apacaẏe biartha muṃ dekhi
<P>pajāite icchā karai muṃ rājyanta upekhi | 58 |
<P>chāḍili māẏāmoha muṃ samasta parityāgī
<P>hoibi bhikṣābāsī nirdwanda parayogī | 59 |
<P>āho mleccha nr̥pati muṃ śiṇili tora bīradhū bānā
<P>śaraṇa macchaḷa kathā kahanti tohora senā | 60 |
<P>mohora prakr̥ti hāde chāceka br̥tti jāṇi
<P>swargadhārākaiṃ āśākali to pratagyāṃ śuṇi | 61 |
<P>śuṇiṇa boilā se meḷaccha nr̥pati
<P>ẏeḍebaḍa dukhī yebe muṃ hoili tora kati | 62 |
<P>nicinteṇa thāasi ẏebe na chaḍa tora rājya
<P>pāṇḍabe samara ye hoilā mora āja | 63 |
<P>āho ājhuṃ tohora thāṭhe senāpati hoantu ye droṇe
<P>daṇḍa gheni pāṇḍabe samare yāāntu teṇe | 64 |
<P>āmbhara sañchita acchi jāḷāndhara bhūagoṭi
<P>śrīkr̥ṣṇaṃku gheniṇa ẏeṇe āsiba kirīṭī | 65 |
<P>āho śrīkr̥ṣṇa arjuna ẏebe samare na thile
<P>chāribhāi pāṇḍabanta jiṇi pāribu ki tohora baḷe | 66 |
<P>driyodhana boilā tu jiṇibu kr̥ṣṇa arjunaku
<P>kṣaṇake jiṇimi muhiṃ chāri pāṇḍabaṃku | 67 |
<P1>65|1 bhua = byuha |
[MBO-08-7]
<P>pūrbe giri durgama pacchime chāripiḍhā
<P>uttare maṇināga dakṣiṇe aṅgirā | 68 |
<P>pañchabiṃśa yojana tahiṃra thaḷa majhi
<P>caukati yamunā saraswatī acchi bhedi | 69 |

<P>bāiśi khaṇā bhitare uṇeiśi pācerī

<P>bijaẏe mānagobinda kurunātha droṇaṃkara sannidhye
<P>droṇakaiṃ senāpati kalā dutīẏa yuddhe | 80 |

<P>ḍhola damālu lakṣeka bhīratūra ḍhāla

<P>bājanti maṅgaḷa mahurī bīṇā śaṅkhadhuni
<P>amarabr̥nda gheni ki bijaẏe sahasra yoni | 91 |
<P>makara śukaḷa pakṣa ẏekādaśī tithi
<P>se dina ārdrā nakṣatra aṭai pāhānti | 92 |
<P>sedina senāpati hoile bhāradwājaṃkara śiṣi
<P>kurukṣetra maṇḍaḷe prabeśa kaleka āsi | 93 |
<P>upāẏe kari guru bhūẏeka rañchilā
<P>catra ākāra kari catrabhūẏeka nirbhākalā | 94 |
<P>baḍai durāpada ārdrābaḷī bhūa rañchi

<P>nabalakṣa rathī pañchiśalakṣa hāthī

<P>ẏeteka saina tule maahāguru droṇa
<P>catrabhūa ābori guru rahile prathama dwāreṇa | 97 |
<P>nabalakṣa aśwa sātalakṣa hāthī daśasahasra rathī
<P>pādānti tinikṣauṇī tule dujadwāre rahilā jadyarathī | 98 |
<P>benilakṣa ratha pāñchalakṣa hāthī caudalakṣa haẏe
<P>sātakṣauṇī pādānti baḷa gheni karṇṇa tijadwāre rahe | 99 |

[MBO-08-10]
<P>chaḍalakṣa ratha ye nabalakṣa hāthī
<P>ẏekādaśa lakṣa aśwa daśakṣauṇī pādānti | 104 |
<P>chaḍadwāre rahile kr̥pa ye āchāryye
<P>tuleṇa achanti tāra tinisasra mahārāje | 105 |
<P>benilakṣa rathī ye pāñchalakṣa hāthī
<P>sātalakṣa aśwa ye sāgare pādānti | 106 |
<P>ẏeteka baḷa gheni bīra aśastamā
<P>saptama dwāre rahilā se chatrīkuḷa uttamā | 107 |
<P>aṣṭama dwārare sātasahasra nr̥pati
<P>saina gheni rahile se māḷabacatrabratī | 108 |
<P>tathi uttāre nabaduāre parabeśa
<P>dhuśāsana tule rahilā aḷambuṣā rākṣasa | 109 |
<P>daśama duāre rahile satarasahasra nr̥pati
<P>saina gheni rahile durddaṇḍa mānacatrabratī | 110 |
<P>lakṣmaṇa kumāra ye mahāmantrī śaṃkuni

<P>pariśa lakṣa ratha chāḷiśa lakṣa maẏemattā
<P>rathī aśwa pādānti ke pāriba gaṇitā | 112 |
<P>asaṃkṣepa saini gheniṇa kurusāiṃ
<P>mahācatra bhedi se rahilā niṭhiāi | 113 |

[MBO-08-11]
<P>catrabhūa dekhiṇa se mānagobinda
<P>droṇaṃkara mukha chāhiṃ se kapoḷe kara dhinda | 114 |
<P>bipāka beḷa mohora ẏeteka kāḷa thilā
<P>melāyuddha kari bhīṣma samasta nāśakalā | 115 |
<P>mānagobinda boilā ẏeheneka buddha tohora thilā yebe guru
<P>ādihuṃ kimpe tuhi ẏe kathā na bichāru | 116 |
<P>muhiṃ āśrija hoili ẏe catrabhūa chāhiṃ
<P>deba dānabe ẏehā bhedite sāmaratha nāhiṃ | 117 |
<P>sādhu sādhu droṇa mahārathī ẏe tohora buddhi

<P>ẏehā śuṇi pucchākale baibasuta manu
<P>mahāpaṇḍita brahmabettā kumbharuṣi tanu | 119 |
<P>jāḷāndhara bhūa rañchile yebaṇamāne
<P>ke ke aṭantise adabhmata āgamane | 120 |
<P>pāṇḍabe airi pacha tāhāṃkara acchi ki pūrbe
<P>kimbhūte jāḷandhara bhūa rañchile prastābe | 121 |
<P>śuṇa ho mahārāja bilaṃka catrabratī
<P>manukāḷa bañchāilu tu śāhāsra saṅgati | 122 |
<P>satyayuge kaṇaẏabindu boli ẏekarāẏe
<P>prāgatīrthe se ye gaṅgāku kale dhyāẏe | 123 |
<P>daśasahasra baraṣa pariyante se ẏekalaẏe bhābi
<P>se rājākaiṃ prasanna hoile jāhnabī | 124 |
<P>dhabaḷa dhauryya śuddha saṣṭika yāhāra kāẏe
<P>triẏambaka mauḷi diśile mahāmaẏe | 125 |
<P>ananta koṭi bhmaja debī tribeṇī saṅgamuṃ
<P>arddhakāẏe birājile kaṇaẏabindu chamu | 126 |
[MBO-08-12]
<P>prasanna hoiṇa āgyāṃ tāku dileka dhabaḷī
<P>bara māga kaṇaẏabindu ye tohore miḷi | 127 |
<P>śuṇiṇa pratibāca se anaṅgasena nāti
<P>prasanna hoilu ki mote abhaẏā pārbatī | 128 |
<P>gaṅgā boile māga ye tohora icchā
<P>māga re kaṇaẏabindu pūroibi manabāñcchā | 129 |
<P>mā go jambudīpa bharathakhaṇḍa aiśānya koṇa deśa

<P>gaṅgā boile tu āga kāṭiyāsi rekhā

<P>kaṇaẏabindu rājā ailā tāhā gheni

[MBO-08-13]
<P>tiniśata yojana tāhāra rājyasthaḷī

<P1>4|2 ``śuṇiṇa mahābhārata pāpa kara dahija'' pāṭha pare kha, ta, dha, nare bhinma pāṭha acchi :--
<P1>catrabhūa goṭi ye rañchile gurudroṇe
<P1>bhedantā nāhiṃ kehi ẏe tini bhmabane ||
<P1>śrīkr̥ṣṇa arjuna ābara padmana bīrahiṃ
<P1>droṇe jāṇanti kebaḷa āna na jāṇanti kehi ||
<P1>jāḷandhara bhūaku arjuna hari yānte
<P1>cintābhare bhāḷanti ye dropatīra kānte ||
<P1>yebaṇa catrabhūa bhedibāku mahīre kehi nāhiṃ
<P1>āmbhara madhye kiẏe samartha aṭai ||
<P1>prathama dwāre achanti droṇa senāpati
<P1>yama kāḷadaṇḍa prāẏa tāṃkara śara śakti ||
<P1>sammukhe miḷante yiba yamaāḷa
<P1>ẏesaneka cintāẏe bhāḷanti dharmabāḷā ||
<P1>ẏesaneka bichārante dharmara nandana
<P1>śrīkr̥ṣṇa caraṇa taḷe āmbhe śaraṇa pañchujana ||
[MBO-08-51]
<P>bhīmasena boile tumbhe śuṇa āho dharmarāẏe
<P>se bhūa bhedibāku sāmartha sinā dhanurjaẏe | 10 |
<P>deba dānabe mānabe gocara hāde nāhiṃ
<P>catrabhūa boli mora śuṇilāta nāhiṃ | 11 |
<P>śuṇiṇa dharmarāẏe pucchanti bāratā
<P>nakuḷa jāṇu kire tu catrabhūara bāratā | 12 |
<P>nakuḷa bolai swāmī dekhilā nāhiṃ naẏane
<P>na paḍhili se bidyā na śuṇilaiṃ karṇṇe | 13 |
<P>puṇa dharmarāẏe pucchanti sahadeba
<P>tumbhe jāṇani kiho se catrabhūara sambhaba | 14 |
<P>sahadeba boile śuṇimā dharmarāẏe
<P>muhiṃ na jāṇaiṃ prahu catrabhūara upāẏe | 15 |
<P>ẏesaneka bichāra karante chāribhrātha
<P>sannidhye prabeśa hoilā āsi arjunara suta | 16 |
<P>chāmure satasahasra daṇḍa pariṇāmi
<P>kimbhūta kāraṇe biṣāde bhāḷucha debaswamī | 17 |
<P>yujheṣṭhi koḷakari dhaile abhimanyu
<P>śuṇare nandana tu sohodrāra tanu | 18 |
<P>śuṇarekumaramaṇi yuddhara āgamana
<P>biṣama yuddha chanda ki kahibi puṇa | 19 |
<P>catrabhūa ẏeka pātichanti gurudroṇa tahiṃ
<P>tāhā bhedibāku kehi na jāṇaiṃ | 20 |
<P>abhimanyu boilā śuṇimā dharmarāẏe
<P>mote mukuṭa bānddha kara ho yoddhāẏe | 21 |
<P>muhiṃ āja catrabhūa bhedibaiṃ raṇe
<P>tumbhe mohora tule thibaṭi chārijaṇe | 22 |
<P>kumāra bacane ye dharmarāẏe hasi
<P>cauda baraṣa agyāna tu bāḷaśiṣi | 23 |
[MBO-08-52]
<P>āmbhe senāpati kehne karibuṭi tote
<P>bhūabheda kathā tu jāṇilu kemante | 14 |
<P>somabaṃśara tu kuḷara maṇḍaṇī dhana mora
<P>tumbhaṃku catrabhūa kathā kāhuṃ se gocara | 15 |
<P>yujheṣṭhi debaṃkara niṣṭhura bākya śuṇi
<P>śuṇa deba dharmarāẏe mohora hāde bāṇī
<P>kahai karayoḍi kumara cūḍāmaṇi | 26 |
<P>swāmī mātāra garbhakāḷe makara śukaḷa traẏodaśī
<P>arkabāra punarbasu nakṣatra mithuna ye rāśi | 27 |
<P>taitiḷa nāme karaṇa āẏuṣmān nāme yoga
<P>se dina pitāmātā heuthile kathā prasaṅga | 28 |
<P>muhiṃ saptamāsa mātā garbhabāsī
<P>mātā pachārile swāmī kathā goṭiẏe kahasi | 29 |
<P>mātāra bacane pitā kahanti dharmaswarūpa kathā
<P>aṅge nirbhāi achanti yeuṃ yeuṃ kathā | 30 |
<P>sohodrā boile swāmī kathāẏe śuṇa tathya
<P>āpaṇe yāhā aṃge nirbhāi śikhi se kathā aṭai tattwa | 31 |
<P>mahābhāratha ye hoiba samara
<P>ẏethira carita deba kebaṇa prakāra | 32 |
<P>śuṇa go subhadre tumbhe kahanti phālaguni
<P>aṣṭādaśa prakāre ye bhūa prabarttinī | 33 |
<P>śakaṭābhūa, padmabhūa, keśara bhūa, sūcībhedabhūa
<P>jāḷandhara bhūa, catrabhūa ādrābaḷī kuṇḍaḷī ye bhūa | 34 |
<P>uluka bhūa ye śahasrabhedi bhūa
<P>gaganabhedi bhūa ghora andhāra ye bhūa | 35 |
<P>mānabhaṅga bhūa bhāluka bhūa barehā ye bhūa
<P>śalyabhūa tribaḷi ābara sāgara ye bhūa | 36 |
<P>aṣṭādaśa bhūa ye ẏesana prakāre
<P>ye yemante bheda hoi kahibā tohora ṭhāre | 37 |
[MBO-08-53]
<P>samasta kahile se mātāṃka samakakṣe
<P>catrabhūara baratā kahile sarbapache | 38 |
<P>pitā kahanteṇa śuṇanti mora māẏe
<P>muhiṃ garbhe thāi tāhā śuṇili dharmarāẏe | 39 |
<P>tr̥tīẏa pahara ye hoilāka rāti
<P>māẏe nidrāgale niśi hoilā pāhānti | 40 |
<P>mātāṃkara nidrāẏe muṃ hoili asāṣṭama
<P>bāhuḍābeḷa bhūaku kali matibhrama | 41 |
<P>yadyapi amaragaṇa tule hari brahmā gheni
<P>bhūa bhedibāra beḷe jiṇi pārai sasrayoni | 42 |
<P>bāhuḍiṇa kemante āsibi na jāṇai buddhi
<P>tahiṃra bāratā na kahile pitā sarbaguṇanidhi | 43 |
<P>mane bichārile yujheṣṭhi dharmanāhā
<P>garbhe thāi jāṇilā ẏe aṭai biṣṇu dehā | 44 |
<P>dhanyare kiriṭī tu pāilu kumara
<P>bhīṣma droṇa tahuṃ ẏe aṭai baḷīẏāra | 45 |
<P>mātā garbha kathā ẏeḍeka sāhasa
<P>ẏeḍe ẏeḍe bacana śuṇi rakhithilu uddeśya | 46 |
<P>yujheṣṭhiṃka bacane bolai abhimanyu
<P>āgyāṃ heu tāta nabhāḷa kicchi manu | 47 |
<P>raṇe catrabhūa mātra pārai muṃ bhedi
<P>kipari bāhuḍibi muṃ kaha mote buddhi | 48 |
<P>abhimanyu mukharu ẏe sana bākya śuṇi
<P>brikodara dhātikāre uṭhilā śira jhuṇi | 49 |
<P1>40|2 ``māẏe nidrāgale niśi hoilā pāhānti'' ehi pāṭha pare ``ja'' pothire adhikā pāṭha :--
<P1>padmabhūa sūcībhūa dwāre nidrāgale
<P1>sehiṭhāru mātā mo śuṇi na pārile |
[MBO-08-54]
<P>bhīmasena boilā bābu na bhāḷa tu tāhā
<P>tera kṣauṇī baḷa gheni muṃ tote hoithibi sāhā | 50 |
<P>bhāñjibu bhūadwāra jiṇimuṃ droṇa karṇṇa
<P>śalya bālahika somadatta driyodhana dhuśāsana | 51 |
<P>āmbhe chāribhrāthe thibuṃ tohora pache
<P>agrate bhūa tu bhedibu pratakṣe | 52 |
<P>ẏeḍe keḍe garutāṇa se kauroba kaicchā
<P>sarila kurubaḷa āja ke karu āsi rakṣā | 53 |
<P>bāhuḍi āsibāku karuchu bābu śaṃkā
<P>ẏethaku kicchi śocanā na kara kumara ẏekā | 54 |
<P>bāhuḍi āsibā beḷaku āsibe kr̥ṣṇa pātha
<P>māribā kauroba baḷa hoibe anāsta | 55 |
<P>abhimanyu boilā deba nakara kicchi cintā
<P>arjuna āsibā yāẏe muhiṃ pāṇḍaba baḷa rakhantā | 56 |
<P>yujheṣṭhi boile bābu satya tu paḷibu
<P>āmbhanta chaḍiṇa bhitare na paśibu | 57 |
<P>prathama duāre sarbe yujhuthibā rahi
<P>arjuna āsibā yāẏe heḷa bujhi tuhi | 58 |
<P>māribi kauroba baḷa dekha tumbhe puṇi
<P>kumāra mukhuṃ ye ẏesana bākya śuṇi
<P>sājile pāṇḍaba sanya ẏekādaśa kṣauṇī | 59 |
<P>tinikoṭi ratha ye pāñchakoṭi hāthī
<P>nabakoṭi turaṅgama nabakṣauṇī pādānti | 60 |
<P>satyayugara sākhā ye ketana sārathi
<P>dhabaḷī nāme ratha maṇḍilā tatakṣaṇānti | 61 |
<P>yujheṣṭhi bhīmasena nakuḷa sahadeba
<P>ẏehānta samārjiṇa kahanti dutīẏa pārthiba | 62 |
<P>sārathiki boilā sāja mohora rahubara
<P>āgyāṃ pramāṇe caḷai se biśwabasura kumara | 63 |
[MBO-08-55]
<P>saṣṭikara caka saṣṭikara chārikhamba
<P>saṣṭikara chāripīḍhā saṣṭikara kalaśa ārambha | 64 |
<P>hīrāra pābaccha ye tathira upare
<P>madhyānaha āditya jāṇi teja parakhare | 65 |
<P>śate śate sari śukaḷa pāṭasūtā
<P>tathire gunthā acchi gajara mukutā | 66 |
<P>saṣṭikara kalaśa upare lambai causarā
<P>jhalakanti caukati māṇikyara jharā | 67 |
<P>tathira upare ye śweta chāmara maṇḍi
<P>markata hīrānīḷā khañjaṇī ratha khaṇḍi | 68 |
<P>sannidhye lambanti jhīna patanī śweta śāḍhī
<P>pāṭa rajjumāna ye tathira dauḍi | 69 |
<P>dhabaḷa śaṅkha śweta gokṣīra chārihaẏe
<P>yesaneke mithuna māse bakapaṃkti prāẏe | 70 |
<P>śaṃkha śweta padma ye gokṣīra chāribarṇṇa
<P>sāñju dei rathe nei yocilā ketana | 71 |
<P>ratha dhabaḷa aśwa ratna dhabaḷa dhabaḷa chāmara dhabaḷa oḷi
<P>se rathara nāma ye aṭai dhabaḷī | 72 |
<P>ādi abatāra se somabaṃśara kuḷe
<P>ādi nama abhimanyura aṭai se bhale | 73 |
<P>satyayuge arathi nāma tāra ketana
<P>dhabaḷī ratha maṇḍiṇa se karai āgamana | 74 |
<P>dāruka dārukī mātaḷi aruṇa
<P>candradhwaja sumanteka ketana nārāẏaṇa | 75 |
<P>ẏeaṣṭa sārathī yuge yuge trijībī
<P>ẏehāṃkara ratha bāhile caḷai madhya pātāḷa ākāśa bhmabi | 76 |
<P1>70|2 yesane mithuna māse āditya udaẏe |(tha, na)
<P1>74|2 se ratha maṇḍilā ye sabu dhabaḷa barṇṇa |(cha, ḍa)
[MBO-08-56]
<P>yadyapi rathimāne līna hoibe kāḷa abasāne
<P>yuge yuge trijībī yehu sārathimāne | 77 |
<P>rathahiṃ akṣaẏe sārathihiṃ akṣaẏe
<P>rathīmāne utapatti hoile sarathiẏe hoanti samaẏe | 78 |
<P>ādityaṃka sārathi aruṇa indra sārathi mātaḷi
<P>kāmadeba sārathi candradhwaja arjuna rathe sarathi deba banamāḷī | 79 |
<P>daśaratha rathe sārathi sumantaka abhimanyu rathe ketana
<P>baḷarāma rathe sarathi daruki dāruka sārathi janārddana | 80 |
<P>mūṃ kisa kahibi ẏe sārathimānaṃka mahimāṃ

<P>chāmure ubhārilā kumāra abhimanyu | 82 |
<P>lakṣeka brāhmaṇa miḷi karanti bedadhuni

<P>tārakā yuddhe yehne kārttikeśwara diśi

<P>dibya beśa aḷaṃkāra ye sohodrāra baḷā
<P>anaṃga abatāra se kr̥ṣṇabarṇṇa kaḷā | 85 |
<P>bairāṣṭara ballabha se guṇasāgara bandhu
<P>pāṇḍabakuḷa rakṣaṇe mahimāṃ yāra sādhu | 86 |
<P>nausahasra baḷa dhanu kareṇa adrābaḷī
<P>duipaṭe aśipadma hīrā jhaḷi | 87 |
<P>pitāmaha srijile yebaṇa dhanu ādi
<P>bhārā nibāraṇe tāhā dileka jambhobhedī | 88 |
<P>ādisr̥ṣṭi sambhaba kāḷe diśanti yehne nirañjana
<P>tesana sārikṣe diśai abhimanya | 89 |
<P1>86|1 śrīkr̥ṣṇaṃkara bhagnījā guṇasāgara sindhu |(kha, na, ṭha)
[MBO-08-57]
<P>dibya abatāra dhari bijaẏa kale rathe
<P>aśwanta maṇḍi ketana basilā saṅgate | 90 |
<P>bāme brikodara ḍāhāṇe nakuḷa
<P>pache sahadeba yujheṣṭhi tule sarbabaḷa | 91 |
<P>pāñchalakṣa yoddhā gheniṇa mahāthāṭhe
<P>āgiāṇi hoichanti dr̥pada birāṭe | 92 |
<P>bājanti bīratūra ṭamaka niśāṇa
<P>caḷanteṇa thāṭha se bhetile gurudroṇa | 93 |
<P>tinisāgara yoddhā gheni prathamadwāre rahichanti droṇaguru
<P>dr̥pada birāṭa dekhi tāṃku rahile khaṇḍadūruṃ | 94 |
<P>jambhodatya bibāde yehne diśanti maghabāne
<P>tesana sādriśe se ye bhāradwādaśaṃkara nandane | 95 |
<P>droṇaṃkara raśmi jāṇi kāḷānaḷa bahani

<P>sārathiki pachārai se kumāra abhimanyu
<P>ketana boila ẏeta bhāradwādaśaṃkara tanu | 97 |
<P>praśurāme pratigrahe samasta bidyā sādhi
<P>ẏehāṃkara bidyāre kurupāṇḍabe mahāyodhī | 98 |
<P>abhimanyu boilā jiṇimā āge ẏehā
<P>bho sārathi ketana mohora dhabaḷī ratha bāhā | 99 |
<P>śaṃkha śweta padma ananta haẏabara chāri
<P>yā yā boile sapatabrathmāṇḍa kṣepipāri | 100 |
<P>yā yā boli āgyāṃ dilāka sārathi
<P>prathame bheṭilā yāiṃ droṇa senāpati | 101 |
<P>ākāśuṃ kṣudratāra yesane paḍanti khasi
<P>nimiṣake droṇaṃka rathaku abhimanyu ratha grāsi | 102 |
<P1>99|2--bho guruketana mohora dhabaḷī ratha bāhā |(ka, ḍa, da, ta, gha)
[MBO-08-58]
<P>adabhmate dekhiṇa pachāranti guru droṇe
<P>pāṇḍabaṃka asamaẏe ki bije kale maẏāṇe | 103 |
<P>droṇaṃka chamuṃre jaṇānti munehiṃ
<P>arjuna nandana abhimanyu aṭai ye ẏehi | 104 |
<P>arjunara tejaru ẏe duguṇa garuhaṃsī
<P>bharadwādaśaṃka nandana bahuta paraśaṃsi | 105 |
<P>droṇaṃkara bichārante ẏeṇe abhimanyu śarakari
<P>pāda sambhāṣaṇe se ghenilā bāṇachāri | 106 |
<P>praḷambite nārāje paḍile droṇa guruṃkara pāde
<P>āśiṣa nārāja droṇe peśileka hāde | 107 |
<P>bichāriṇa droṇe mati kale bhraṣṭa

<P>ẏesanaka bichāra karante droṇaguru

<P>droṇa apasari gale bāḷaka bolikari
<P>mukuḷā pāi sanya aneka se māri | 112 |

<P>pāñchalakṣa yoddhā paḍante droṇa baḷa bhāji

<>boile adharma yuddha ẏehā tule mahāśrama |(ca)
<P1>115|2--bhūabheda karāilu re droṇa durmati |(ṭha)
[MBO-08-59]
<P>śuṇiṇa bikarāḷa droṇa bidyāguru
<P>bāḷuta kumara boli āmbhe ye heḷayuddha kalu | 116 |
<P>basilāke mahāroṣa daṇḍabhagna dekhi
<P>binddhale nārāja guru uprodha upekṣa | 117 |
<P>bajrasārikṣe ye pañchadaśa bāṇa
<P>kope binddhale ye mahāguru droṇa | 118 |
<P>yesaneke ākāśu paḍai giribara
<P>sehi sādr̥śe garji bāṇa paḍanti upara | 119 |
<P>bhūabheda nārāja se aṭe tīkṣamunā

<P>se anaḷa tīkhabaṇa sārathi aṃge bhedi

<P>samare prahāra kale aneka saini | 128 |
<P1>119 yesaneka kāḷasarpa paśai bimbare
<>tesane paḍante śara cchedai mumare ||
[MBO-08-60]
<P>medamedā māṃsare pr̥thī hoilā karddana
<P>gahaḷa dhandoḷa ye bārita na galā sanya | 129 |
<P>droṇaṃkara samara sahilā bīra abhimanyu
<P>bhīmasenakaiṃ ke achai abā samānu | 130 |
<P>kr̥tāntaka jiṇī tāhāra teja ye bikāśi

<P>br̥ndāraka deśara rājā madanasena nr̥pati

<P>droṇaṃkara tule ye thile śasra gheni

<P>gajanta dhariṇa se kachāḍilā bhīma

<P>bāmakare gadāẏeka prahāra kalā toḷi

<P>aśisahasra yoddhā aśisahasra matta hāthī

<H>{@abhimanyura ẏekādaśa dwāra bheda o abhimanyu badha@}
<P>ẏethu anantare jāḷandhara bhūa kathā
<P>munehi dile nei pāṇḍabanta bāratā | 1 |
<P>swāmī abadhāri śuṇimā yujheṣṭhi rājadeba
<P>jāḷandhara pañchadwāra jaẏa kaleni pārthiba | 2 |
<P>swāmī caurāśi lakṣa ye meḷakṣa yoddhā thile
<P>pāñchadwāre deba caubana lakṣa yoddhā paḍile | 3 |
<P>swāmī kāli dibasa rātre bicitra sāṃgrāma
<P>rātra dibasa na jāṇiluṃ kṣaṇe nāhiṃ biśrama | 4 |

<P>mārante na saranti se dr̥bhāra danuja | 5 |
<P>tāhāṃkara rudhira deba paḍanteṇa kṣiti
<P>mandāke śate danuja hoanti utapatti | 6 |
<P>swāmī ẏebeheṃ hoilāni āsi deḍharahara beḷā

<P>nanddhaghoṣa kr̥ṣṇa sārathi nāhiṃ, nāhiṃ kapiketana dhwaja cinha | 65 |
<P>bichārai bhāroimalla dhabaḷīratha dekhi
<P>karatāra bijaẏe kale ki śūnyabhmabana upekṣi | 66 |

<P>tote kehne samare peṣilere pāmare | 70 |

<P>abaśya prāṇa nāśi samare yehu paśi | 71 |

[MBO-08-81]
<P>kebaṇa abhimāna pāilusi re bāḷa
<P>bichadoi sāṃgrāme kimpe paśilure chāṇḍāḷa | 74 |
<P>keneha gobinda re tumbhanta saṃpakṣa
<P>thāṭha sanya ādikari kehi nāhānti tora pacha | 75 |
<P>kheḷantā hasantā ture aṭu bāḷuta hāde pua

<P>prahtama dwāra rakhanti ye rāẏe guru droṇe

<P>bābu tohora saṃkalpakure sabuṃkari āśa
<P>kimbhūta bairāgare tu samare dilu jhāsa | 85 |

[MBO-08-83]
<P>āho caitana gurujana jhiṃghāsa śuṇi kopita abhimanyu

<P>bhāratha yuddhe abhimanyu thiba yetedina pariyante
<P>arjunaku ubhākari nuāribe jagannāthe | 454 |
<P>ẏe bhāratha yuddhe uprodha na chaḍiba bīrapātha
<P>kaurobaṃka saṃge abhimanyu yuddha kari bratibā paryyanta | 455 |
<P>kaurobanta sodrimāpaṇa pāḷicchi pāṃlaguni
<P>putrakaṣṭe māriba se sakaḷa kauraba baḷa saini | 456 |
<P1>454|2 ubhākari--ṭhiākari |
<P1>456|2 ``putrakaṣṭe māriba se sakaḷa kauroba baḷa saini'' :--ehi pāṭha
<>pare ``cha'' pothire adhika pāṭha :--
<P1>abhimanyu male teṇe jāḷandhara jiṇime
<P1>kaurobe maribe ye ajunara tame |
<P1>ẏemanta bhiāṇa hari āgahuṃ se kari
<P1>br̥haspatiṃka chamure bāsaba pachāri |
<P1>bho guru udekabandha swarga kala jūra
<P1>āmbhe tāku raṇe sari nohu debāsura |
<P1>ye duṣṭa drapiṣṭa āne kemante mariba
<P1>br̥haspati boile kahibā tahiṃra bhāba |
<P1>ādi janma hoilā ye se hodrā garbhare
<P1>bihantāpuruṣa peṣi tāhānta gheniāsa
<P1>se ādi udekabandhaku karibaṭi nāśa |
<P1>āja yadi na āsiba amara maṇḍaḷe
<P1>kāli kr̥ṣṇa arjunaku māriba samare |
<P1>ẏehā śuṇi surarāẏe hoile uṣata
<P1>takṣaṇe peṣidile bihantā puruṣanta |
<P1>āhe bihantā puraṣe yahuṃ kale kūṭakapaṭa
<P1>nārāja bindhante hoilā akāṭa apuṭa |
[MBO-08-112]
<P>udekabandha nāśayiba kr̥ṣṇa arjuna hoiba

<P1>576|1 gataātmā prāẏe hoile śūnye ratha chāhiṃ |(tha, ña)
<P1>578--sahadebakaiṃ boile mahīpati
<>hāribā jiṇimā se kṣatrīṃkara br̥tti ||(ca, ga)
[MBO-08-122]
<H>{@sañjaẏa dhr̥tarāṣṭraṅkara kathopakathana
<>o
<>arjunara aśubha darśana@}
<P>āho teṇe jaẏaśaṃkha dhuni kariṇa hastinā paśanti kuruthāṭha
<P>sañjaẏe hakāriṇa pucchai dhr̥tirāṣṭa | 1 |
<P>āho baḍāi utsabata āmbhara saini
<P>jaẏeśaṃkha maṃgaḷa ta śubhai ghora dhuni | 2 |
<P>śatr̥jita pātāṅga uḍai sabuṃkari rathara upare
<P>bhīma paḍilā ki āho ājara samare | 3 |
<P>teṇukari utsaba se hoikinā āmbhara thāṭha
<P>bhīma kṣaẏegale nicaḷa mohora pañchurāṣṭa | 4 |
<P>jadyaratha ye sebā karithilā deba kāśī
<P>arjuna na thile chāripāṇḍabanta pārai se naśi | 5 |
<P>jāḷandhara bhūaku hari ghenigale arjunaku
<P>nicaẏe jadyaratha nāśa kalāṭi chāri pāṇṭabaṃku | 6 |
<P>jadyaratha nāẏeṃ śubhmacchiki jaẏe jaẏe bāṇī
<P>sadhu puṇyabantī mohora duśilā dulanī | 7 |
<P>ẏemanta śubhayoge jadyarathakaiṃ muṃ dilāiṃ kumārī
<P>kāḷe mote hoilā se parama hitakārī | 8 |
<P>sañjaẏe boile śuṇa ho bicitrabīryyara santati
<P>catrabhūa bhiāile se droṇa senāpati | 9 |
<P>arjunaku gheni hari gale bhūa jāḷandhare
<P>abhimanyu senāpati hoilā ājara samare | 10 |
<P>prathama dūāre jiṇilā se gurudroṇaṃku
<P>chāripāṇṭabe abhimanyu paśile ho bhitaraku | 11 |
<P>duja duāre sindhurāja jadyaratha thilā
<P>iśwara bara prasāde se chāripāntabanta ogāḷilā | 12 |
<P>duja dwāra jiṇi ẏekā galā abhimanyu
<P>ratha nāma dhabaḷī sārathi nāma ketanu | 13 |
[MBO-08-123]
<P>śaṅkhaśwetapadma mahāpadma haẏe chāri
<P>karṇṇara tule hoilā aneka dwandakārī | 14 |
<P>karṇṇakaiṃ jiṇilā se tijadwāre paśi
<P>śalyaṃku jiṇilā se caturthadwāre āsi | 15 |
<P>bhūrisarbaṃku jiṇilā pañchama duāre
<P>kr̥paṃku ṣaṣṭhe jiṇilā bāḷuta kumare | 16 |
<P>saptame aśastamā jiṇilāka tame
<P>aṣṭame somadatta jiṇilā sāṃgrāme | 17 |
<P>nabame kaurobanta jiṇilā kumara
<P>aneka hāthī rathī paḍile samare | 18 |
<P>nabamadwāra jiṇi catrabhūa galā bhedi
<P>nārāje koṭi koṭi pādānti yoddhā cchedi | 19 |
<P>daśasahasra rājā aśi sahasra rathī
<P>gajaaśwa yoddhā tinisāgara pāñchapadma pādānti | 20 |
<P>chattāra bādyakāra paḍile pāñchakoṭi
<P>ẏekā ẏeteka dhaṃsilā se bāḷuta puagoṭi | 21 |
<P>jiṇita nuārile se yugata samare
<P>kapaṭa yuddhakari beḍhi māile bāḷuta kumare | 22 |
<P>samaste beḍhi bhīmāku pārante yebe māri
<P>nicaẏe pañchu rājye ho hoantānā adhikārī | 23 |
<P>sañjaẏe boilā rājā śuṇibā dhr̥tirāṣṭa
<P>abhimanyu nidhane tote hoiba putrakaṣṭa | 24 |
<P>anekabāra jiṇaiṃ arjuna tohora putraṃku
<P>prāṇe na mārai ẏekā se uprodha karai tumbhaṃku | 25 |
<P>mohaśare bindhai ye prāṇe na mārai pāṭha
<P>bolai ẏehākara male andha pitāgoṭi hoiba anātha | 26 |
<P1>21|1 chatradhara bādyakāra paḍile pāñchakoṭi |(bahupāṭha)
<P1>21|2 chattāra--chaatāra biśiṣṭa bādya biśeṣa |
[MBO-08-124]
<P>ẏeteka uprodha tohroa puaṃku thilā dhr̥tirāṣṭa
<P>ẏebe dekhibunā ho tohora putrakaṣṭa | 27 |
<P>ẏebe moha chaḍiba pātha putrara nidhane
<P>ājhuṃ aputrika hoiluṭi jāṇithā tora mane | 28 |
<P>sañjaẏe boilā mohora bichāraku na yogāi ẏe utsaba
<P>mote diśuacchi sabu ẏe biccheda swabhāba | 29 |
<P>sañjaẏe mukharu śuṇi nirāpaẏe bārata
<P>bāḷuta putraku māri mora poẏe manare ẏeḍeka uṣata | 30 |
<P>abhimanyu nipāte mohora kuḷahiṃ buḍilā
<P>lakṣaṇakumāra bratai kire dhr̥tirāṣṭa boilā | 31 |
<P>abhimanyu nidhana boli śubhilā hastināre
<P>robanti tirīgaṇe miḷi anteśwara pure | 32 |
<P>bibidha biḷāpa se karanti tirīgaṇe
<P>rūpa bāunanti robanti ki samudra ghoṣaṇe | 33 |
<P>dhr̥tirāṣṭa biṣāda karilā tāhā śuṇi
<P>hr̥dagate bichāra se karai puṇa puṇi | 34 |
<P>hastinā rājyara ẏesaneka bāratā
<P>śuṇimā sabadhāne ẏebe pāṇṭabaṃka kathā | 35 |
<P>biṣāda ātmā hoi galeka chāribhāi
<P>indrapraśaste prabeśa hoile bege yāiṃ | 36 |
<P>badaẏanti agasti śuṇa baibasuta manu
<P>jāḷandhara bhūa teṇe bhedile kr̥ṣṇa pāṃlagunyu | 37 |
<P>abhimanyu nipāta jāṇile dhyāneṇa debahari
<P>jāḷandhara bhūa takṣaṇe ghaḍike saṃhāri | 38 |
<P>tiniśata rājana nabasāgara yodhī
<P>pāñchakṣauṇī baḷa ẏekā arjuna binddha | 39 |
<P>arjunakaiṃ hari ye māẏā karithile
<P>rakatabīryya prāẏe sanya mārante na sarile | 40 |
[MBO-08-125]
<P>abhimanyu nidhana galā yetebeḷe
<P>jāḷandhara bhūahiṃ ẏeṇe sarilā abaheḷe | 41 |
<P>jaẏatu yogeśwara jagata sodara nāhā
<P>māẏadhara puruṣa na jāṇai abā kāhā | 42 |
<P>nirmaḷa jaḷe yenhe bihaḍanti haṃsapanti
<P>hr̥dagate bighasu mora śrīkr̥ṣṇa śuddha jyoti | 43 |
<P>buḍilā sakaḷa dharma akāraṇa mohalāgi
<P>bākyadebīra bhaṇḍāra bidhwaṃsili mohora bhāgī | 44 |
<P>akāda sagata saṃsāra ẏe mohajaḷa pāṃśi
<P>jagabandana nātha motetaba bhmabana diasi | 45 |
<P>atimāẏāre māẏādhara se yāhāra nāma
<P>śrīkr̥ṣṇa caraṇe mohora śatasahasra daṇḍa pariṇāma | 46 |
<P>swāmī abhāba saṃsāra muṃ dekhili anīti
<P>jība hou ki ajība hou tohore paramagati | 47 |
<P>sadaẏe dhāraṇa nātha saẏaḷa janacintā
<P>nāśakara daṇḍaru nātha tuhi se uddharantā | 48 |
<P>yadyapi bhajili nātha mana bacana karttabye
<P>ẏe nirāpekṣa dwandaru mote pārikaribā bāsudebe | 49 |
<P>na dekhili na paḍhili na śuṇili na bhābili mamahr̥de
<P>kiñchita bhābaku muṃ ye pāili śabade | 50 |
<P>hr̥daẏaku aḷaṃkāra mora śrīkr̥ṣṇa nāmagoṭi
<P>taba padmapāde mor aśira kamaḷa loṭi | 51 |
<P>nīḷa utpaḷa jiṇi ye baṇa kandara
<P>manukāḷa bañchāila nātha tahiṃra upara | 52 |
<P1>44--buḍilā saṃsāra ẏe mohajaḷe akāraṇa
<>bakyadebīra bhaṇḍāra muṃ kalāiṃ bidhwaṃsana |(ña, ja, tha)
<P1>48|1 ẏe bhaba saṃsāra nātha saẏaḷa janacintā |(ka, ña, ṅa, tha, jha)
<P1>48|2 durāpada dwandaru nātha tuhi se uddharantā |(ka, ṅa, tha)
<P1>52|1 nīḷasundara nāma yebaṇa kandara |(ṅa, na, ṭha)
[MBO-08-126]
<P>saẏaḷa jana cintāmaṇi puruṣaṃka uttama
<P>hr̥dagate bhābuthāi mohora śrīrāma śrīkr̥ṣṇa nāma | 53 |
<P>tuḷusāra ballabha śrīcaraṇa hr̥dagate mama dhyāna
<P>śūdramuni sāroḷā dāsa praṇapatya pratidina | 54 |
<P>badaẏanti agasti śuṇa baibasuta manu
<P>sātukīki chahiṃ āgyāṃ dle dharmaṃkara tanu | 55 |
<P>tu mohora bacana śuṇasi hāde bābu
<P>jāḷandhara bhūayāẏe ẏehikṣaṇi yibu | 56 |
<P>durāpada samara teṇe karai arajuna
<P>ẏeṇe nidhana hoile kumāra abhimanyu | 57 |
<P>na puṇa bāratā tahiṃ pāi pāṃlaguni
<P>putrakaṣṭe prāṇa puṇa naāsai gheni | 58 |
<P>putra bināśa boli yemante najāṇu kirīṭī
<P>na puṇa indra praśastaku naāsai leuṭi | 59 |
<P>bho dharmadebatā kehi na kahu arjuna āgare
<P>sehi bāṭe napuṇa pātha paśai samare | 60 |
<P>kahuṃ kahuṃ trodhita se dharma mahīpati
<P>ha hā nandana boli paḍi mohayānti kṣiti | 61 |
<P>tu mohora nandana re prāṇara pañchabhūta
<P>kuḷara maṇḍanamora anāthara nātha | 62 |
<P>somabaṃśaku uddhāraṇa aṭu ture batsā
<P>budilāka baṃśa mohora ke kariba rakṣā | 63 |
<P>puṇa puṇa naranātha paḍanti mahīloṭi
<P>ke mohora nibāila kuḷara dīpagoṭi | 64 |
<P>yujheṣṭhiṃki koḷakari robai bhīmasena
<P>kebaṇakati chaḍigalu re bāḷuta kumara abhimanya | 65 |
<P1>63--somabaṃśaku dhāraṇa bābu tuhi se kalpataru
<>buḍilā somabaṃśa kehi nāhiṃ uddhāru |(ka, ña, tha)
[MBO-08-127]
<P>bīrabara sundara tu kaicchā jagajjeṭhī
<P>pr̥thīki aḷaṃkāra re tohora nāmagoṭi | 66 |
<P>nirlaja ātmā bābure bratibāra kisaartha
<P>abaśya prāṇa bisarjibi muṃ khāibaiṃ biṣa | 67 |
<P>poḍu poḍu ātmā mohora ẏehikṣaṇi yāu
<P>bhāira āsibā yāẏe prāṇa mo śarīre nathau | 68 |
<P>celika pua mora nāśagalā mohora dekhante
<P>kisa boli arjuna āsi bolibaṭi mote | 69 |
<P>robai bhīmasena bhūmireṇa paḍi
<P>jaḷu ẏe śarīra boli pāṣāṇe śira koḍi | 70 |
<P>yuga antakāḷa āsi hoilā mukui
<P>tote marāi bābure bratiacchi muhiṃ | 71 |
<P>bho daiba puruṣa mora jaḷu beni ākhi
<P>muhiṃ nirlaja rahili tohora bināśa dekhi | 72 |
<P>kisa śabada śubhiba ẏe sāṃsārikā dharme
<P>pāṇṭabe thāānte abhimanyu paḍilā sāṃgrāme | 73 |
<P>saṃsāre apakhyāti kāpuruṣa boli gaṇi
<P>karate kāṭi muṇḍa prāṇa bisarjibi ẏehikṣaṇi | 74 |
<P>kiṃpāiṃ rahichu re ẏe nirlaja pañchabhūta ātmā
<P>śarīruṃ chaḍi bege yāasi ho mahātamā | 75 |
<P>ohokuḷaku mohora tu ẏekai putragoṭi
<P>kemante prāṇa dhariba śuṇile mo bhāi kiraṭī | 76 |
<P>nakuḷara trodha ye kahita ki pāri
<P>pāṣāṇa upare nei nija ura śira tāḍi | 77 |
<P>hā hā nandanare kuḷara śreṣṭhasāra
<P>āmbhanta chaḍi āga hoila apahāra | 78 |
<P1>69|2--celika--theḷantā śiśu |
[MBO-08-128]
<P>bābu āmbhe tote ghenigalu mukuṭa yoddhāpaṇe
<P>tote se dei āmbhe ailu chārijaṇe | 79 |
<P>bābu kisa kāraṇare āu jībana āmbhara
<P>bāḷuta putra marāi āmbhe bratilu pāmara | 80 |
<P>janamukha chāhiṃ kesane bratiboṅgu nirlaja
<P>chatrīkuḷe dūṣaṇa āmbhanta baḍalāja | 81 |
<P>trodhe baikula yenhe paḍai bajraghāta
<P>gataātmā prāẏe bhūmire paḍita | 82 |
<P>sagadeba jiKajaru dgaruccgu yujheṣṭhiṃki
<P>ābara kuḷadīpa pāibi kāhiṃ dekhi | 83 |
<P>bāhāreṇa sāṣṭama ye bhītareṇa baḍa bathā
<P>dharaṇī pāṃṭuacchi yujheṣṭhiṃka byathā | 84 |
<P>anamite dwandare paśilu rājyabhāra poḍu poḍu
<P>putrakaṣṭa pāra hoibā pañchuprāṇa chadu | 85 |
<P>dahai troṭānaḷa pañchubhūta ātmā
<P>lokite sāṣṭama se mahārājā mahātamā | 86 |
<P>abhimanyu samare paḍilā yetebeḷe
<P>śūnya bhmabana tejiṇa gale daśadiga pāḷe | 87 |
<P>āditya astagala chaḍadaṇḍa thāuṃ dibasa
<P>medinī daladalita andhāra ghora daśadiśa | 88 |
<P>ākāśuṃ khasi ki paḍile ratipati
<P>yugāntaka kāḷaprāẏe diśai nabadīpā pr̥thī | 89 |
<P>somabaṃśa uddhāraṇa yebaṇa putragoṭi
<P>tāhāra nidhane kari leuṭilā nabasr̥ṣṭi | 90 |
<P1>81--kṣetrī kuḷaku dūṣaṇa baḍalāja
<>jana mukhe apakhyāti kuḷeṇa hīnabīryya |(keteka pothi)
<P1>85|2--putra kaṣṭa dekhi prāṇa kimpe ho na chaḍu |(ka, ṇa)
[MBO-08-129]
<P>pr̥thibī dīpa prāẏe putra yahuṃ nāśagalā
<P>ulukāpāta jāṇi caudiga diśilā | 91 |
<P>diga andhara dekhi pucchai pāṃlaguni
<P>catrabrateka hoi bulai bhmabana tini | 92 |
<P>swamī āja ye makaramāsa śakaḷa traẏodaśa tithi
<P>nija rūpa dharita na diśilā niśāpati | 93 |
<P>āditya debatā astagalā beḷa thāuṃ
<P>ẏeherṇṇaka aniryāpa bikāśila deba kāhuṃ | 94 |
<P>gobinde boile pātha sāṃgrāma gahaḷe
<P>reṇu uḍanteṇa gagane na diśile digapāḷe | 95 |
<P>aneka brāhmaṇa chāṇḍāḷa ẏekayoge raṇe mari
<P>pāpa bādhā basai dharmayuddha yahuṃ sari | 96 |
<P>tahiṃ nimante ẏemāne diśanti anādr̥ṣṭi
<P>samra bolikari yehu uttama araṣṭi | 97 |
<P>chāḍilā manabhrānti sohodrāra nāhā
<P>hari kurukṣetra maṇḍaḷaku mora ratha bāhā | 98 |
<P>arjunara bacane se deba madhuhārī
<P>raṇabhūmire prabeśa ye rātra daṇḍachāri | 99 |
<P>dekhanti ratha, gaja, aśwa, pādāntiṃkara piṇḍa
<P>cchidraprāẏe hoi cchiḍi paḍichanti khaṇḍa khaṇḍa | 100 |
<P>pañchayojana pariyante karddana rakata māẏeṃsa
<P>bihaḍanti niśācare preta ye pichāśa | 101 |
<P1>95|2--reṇu uḍanteṇa na diśile dibākare |(gha, ṭa)
<P1>96--aneka brāhmaṇa chāṇḍāḷa raṇe dhwaṃsi
<>hatyāra doṣa ye śarīreṇa diśi |(ṭa, ña)
<P1>97|1--tahiṃ nimante ẏemāne diśanti āna dr̥ṣṭi |(ja, ga, jha)
<P1>100|2--cchinnachantra prāẏe hoi paḍichanti khaṇḍa khaṇḍa |(ja, ṭha)
[MBO-08-130]
<P>brāgha bhāluka śrīkāḷa kāka śāguṇā ulūka
<P>kiḷikiḷā śabada ye huanti utsuka | 102 |
<P>chamaṇḍā chacikā ye ḍākiṇī bhairobī
<P>yoginī kaṃkāḷī betāḷī ruṇḍa sarbadebī | 103 |
<P>keśa mukuḷa bibasana bikaṭa bikarāḷī
<P>meda medā māṃse keḷi kutuhoḷi | 104 |
<P>medinī dala dalita laha laha jihwā matuāḷī
<P>khepanti nācanti gābanti dyanti huḷahuḷi | 105 |
<P>dekhiṇa sānanda ye pārthiba dhanañjaẏe
<P>bhīmasena ṭhākuraṃkara ẏesaneka upāẏe | 106 |
<P>arjuna bolai swāmī śuṇimā yadukuḷa nāhā
<P>pachāribā samare ke māilā kāhā kāhā | 107 |
<P>bāhuḍāi ratha bāhile debaswāmī
<P>kr̥ṣṇa arjuna duheṃ chadile raṇa bhūmi | 108 |
<P>āsante kr̥ṣṇaṃku pucchai dhanurjaẏe
<P>bāma naẏana mora puṃrai debarāẏe | 109 |
<P>hr̥daẏa biṣāda mora baikulya pañchabhūta
<P>maṅgaḷata na diśai mote ẏe tini jagata | 110 |
<P>bāmeṇa śabada karai uluka pacchī
<P>āgeṇa biikarāḷa bobi diai jambukī | 111 |
<P>adabhūte naẏanu mo bahai aśr̥ bāri
<P>trodheṇa gāṇḍima dhanu muṃ nuārai dhari | 112 |
<P>pramāda diśai mote byākuḷe pañchuātmā
<P>kebaṇa māẏā bhiāṇa karicha ho mahatamā | 113 |
<P>chāribhai mora paḍile ki raṇe
<P>catrabhūa kūṭa kapaṭa ki kale gurudroṇe | 114 |
<P>hari śukhilā kāṣṭha dāḷa upare basikari kāka
<P>bikaṭāḷa karita āge diai ghora ḍāka | 115 |
[MBO-08-131]
<P>gobinde boile pātha dwandare paśile
<P>yaśa apayaśa thāiki tohora bole | 116 |
<P>gobinde boile yadyapi āsanti brahmā rudra indra
<P>tohora bhaiṃki nāhiṃ kebehaṃ pramāda | 117 |
<P>utupāta kāḷa yetebeḷe hoithāi pātha
<P>mandakathāmāna heuthāiṃ ye bahuta | 118 |
<P>apāra aśubha dekhanti pāṃlaguni
<P>kūṭe bañchāi āsanti śrīkr̥ṣṇa ye gheni | 119 |
<P>sātukī ḍākadila mahābāta parbatare uṭha
<P>paṇḍabaṃku biyoga deba āsa bege leuṭi | 120 |
<P>sātukī śrīkr̥ṣṇākaiṃ saṃketa deigalā
<P>agyāne arjuna tahā ye maṇita na galā | 121 |
<P>indrapraśaste yāiṇa prabeśa ye hoile tatakṣaṇa
<P>dekhile bhmabana ye diśai amaṅgaḷaṇa | 122 |
<P>stirīẏe bidhabā yenhe bhrathāra bihune
<P>sehi sārikṣe diśanti rājya sarbajane | 123 |
<P>yeteka jana se dekhai sarbasacī
<P>uṣata ullāsa ye kāhāri nāhiṃ kicchi | 124 | [1471 + 124 = 1595]
<H>{@pāṇḍabādiṅka biḷāpa@}
<P>bāhāra mandire bije dharmasuta
<P>ratharu ohlāi ye gamanti kr̥ṣṇa pāṭha | 1 |
<P>yujheṣṭhaṃki ārādhana karanti puṇa beni
<P>sodaranta dekhi bhrānti phiṭilā pāṃlaguni | 2 |
<P1>118|2--apāra biparīta diśai asuārtha |--bahu pāṭha |
[MBO-08-132]
<P>mastake hāthadei pucchai dhanurjaẏe
<P>swāmī catrabhūara kathā kaha kebaṇa upāẏe | 3 |
<P>apāra pratagyāṃ ye karithile gurudroṇe
<P>sāṃgrāme paḍile keuṃ keuṃ rājāgaṇe | 4 |
<P>kesaneka catrabhūa pārila tumbhe bhedi
<P>samare aneka ye paḍichanti yodhī | 5 |
<P>apāra purasari ye pucchai dhanurjaẏe
<P>trodhabhare kicchi kahi nuāranti dharmarāẏe | 6 |
<P>arjuna boile ye prathama dwāre thile gurudroṇe
<P>tāhākaiṃ jiṇimaku ke sāmaratha hoilāka raṇe | 7 |
<P>duja dwāreṇa ye thile rāẏa jadyaratha
<P>pāṇḍabanta jiṇima boli bara deichanti biśwanātha | 8 |
<P>ke samaratha hoilā tāhanta jiṇimāku
<P>ke āne jiṇilā karṇṇa, śalya, kr̥pa, bhūrisarbaṃku | 9 |
<P>bhīmasena boilā bābure śuṇa sarbasācī
<P>abheda catrabhūa dekhi āmbhanta na puṃrilā kicchi | 10 |
<P>abhimanyu boila ẏehā pārai muhiṃ bhedi
<P>bāhuḍi āsibāra kara tumbhe buddhi | 11 |
<P>āmbhe bichārilu bāhuḍi āsibāra beḷe
<P>kr̥ṣṇa arajuna āsi huanti sinā roḷe | 12 |
<P>prathama dwāre ẏekā nārājeka binddha
<P>droṇaṃkara haẏe sārathi dhanutroṇa cchedi | 13 |
<P>hāboḍā śare yahuṃ paḍileka droṇaguru
<P>aneka yodddhānta paśi māilu bhitaru | 14 |
<P>duja dwāreṇa samara ye jadyaratha tule
<P>abhimanyu śahasre tinisahasra rājā paḍile | 15 |
<P>bhaẏakari jadyaratha dwāra chaḍigalā
<P>abhimanyu bhitare paśante āmbhanta ogāḷilā | 16 |
[MBO-08-133]
<P>ẏekā kumāra se galā ratha bāhi
<P>tijadware ho hāde karṇṇa acchi rahi | 17 |
<P>aneka yuddha bābu ho kalā tāhāra tule
<P>abhimanyura bighāte aneka yoddhā paḍile | 18 |
<P>karṇṇaku biartha kari galā abhimanyu
<P>śalya kr̥paku jiṇilā tohora ye tanu | 19 |
<P>bhūrisarba aśastamā aḷambuṣa somadatta kāśī kauśika
<P>daśasahasra rājā tule saini aneka | 20 |
<P>ẏemante nabadwāra kumara galā jiṇi
<P>ẏeka ẏeka nārāje koṭi koṭi hāṇi | 21 |
<P>ẏeke ẏeke samareṇa yahuṃ nuārile jiṇi
<P>adharma goḷayuddha ye sampādile āṇi | 22 |
<P>pāñchakharba rathī gheni āpaṇe kururāẏe
<P>beḍhiṇa māile tora bāḷuta tanaẏe | 23 |
<P>bhīmasena boilā ẏekā jadyaratha prasāde
<P>abhimanyu prāṇatyāja hoilāka hāde | 24 |
<P>bhīmasena mukhuṃ ẏesaneka bākya śuṇi
<P>paḍilā dhanurjaẏe bajraghāta jāṇi | 25 |
<P>asāṣṭame acebana hoi paḍilā bibaccha
<P>koḷakari tāhākaiṃ dhaile śrībatsa | 26 |
<P>mukhare śītaḷa jaḷa ye cchiñchanti acyuta
<P>sāṣṭāma hoi trodha karai bīrapātha | 27 |
<P>hā hā nandanare mora jagu sodara bābu
<P>prāṇabāndhaba mora pañchabhūta ātmā sabu | 28 |
<P>āre kebaṇa pātaka muṃ karithili pūrbe
<P>tahiṃki śāpa mote bihilā daibe | 29 |
<P1>22|2--adharma yuddhakari sanddhale śara āṇi |(ka, tha, ṭa)
<P1>24|1--prasāde--saṅge |
[MBO-08-134]
<P>muhiṃ tohore putrare na gali niuchaṇā
<P>somabaṃśa uddhāraṇa re mora kuḷara dulaṇā | 30 |
<P>puṇa puṇa arjuna ye paḍai bajra ghāte
<P>nirghātabāṇa āsi paḍu mora māthe | 31 |
<P>arjunara trodha dekhi deba ye ananta
<P>garbheṇa ānanda bāhāre kāndanti jagannātha | 32 |
<P>bābu yadukuḷa candramā re ke nelāka hari
<P>kebaṇa bāpuḍā mora janme janme bairi | 33 |
<P>akāḷa bākya āsi hoilāka mote
<P>nanda yāśodāṃka mukha muṃ chāhiṃbi kemante | 34 |
<P>ye deba māẏāẏeṇa sakaḷa jana prabodhi
<P>bhitareṇa sānanda ye bāhāreṇa mahātrodhī | 35 |
<P>arjunara trodha ye kahile na sarai
<P>pr̥thī pāṃṭuacchi mohaghāte paḍai | 36 |
<P>bābu śūrabanta sundara kaicchā jagajjeṭhī
<P>ākāśare paḍai tohora nāmagoṭi | 37 |
<P>bipadakāḷa āsi paḍilā re mote
<P>putra nāśagalā ẏebe pitāra dekhante | 38 |
<P>bābu śarada pūrṇṇimā candra jāṇi tora mukha
<P>siṃhikāra nandana ki tote dhaṃsila pratakṣa | 39 |
<P>bābu ākuñchita keśa śohābana tora
<P>ẏekakhaṇḍa kapāḷa candramā cakora | 40 |
<P>ārakta benilocana khagabara nāsā
<P>kebaṇa pātake putra re tora na pāili āśā | 41 |
<P>abalokana chāhāṃṇi kiñchita beni dr̥ṣṭi
<P>āre tohora bihune mora pañchaprāṇa yāu phuṭi | 42 |

<P1>32|2--śokajaḷe bhāsi ākuḷa pañchu bhūta |(cha)
<P1>42|2--munigaṇa hr̥de chāhānte madanabāṇe puṃṭi |(ca, ka, ta, ṅa, dha)
[MBO-08-135]
<P>paṃku bimbaphaḷa oṣṭha hīrā dantapanti
<P>tohora apāda putrare paḍu mohora hr̥dagati | 43 |
<P>bābu jhaṭakanti kuṇḍaḷa śobhanti beni karṇṇa
<P>mukui prāpata nohilu putra poḍu mora karma | 44 |
<P>kunda ghaṭaṇa jāṇi tohora gaṇḍamaṇḍaḷa
<P>bitramasiṃgha jāṇi ātraṣaṇa bakṣasthaḷa | 45 |
<P>praḷamba sundara re tohora benibāhā
<P>atulāita putra re bāunimi tora kāhā | 46 |
<P>rakata kumuda jāṇi tohora beni karasthaḷī
<P>ghaṭaṇa poẏeḷā jāṇi tohora aṅguḷi | 47 |
<P>yāipākhuḍā jāṇi tohora laha saṃjāta
<P>tohora apāda paḍure mohora mātha | 48 |
<P>babu ātraṣaṇa bistāra tohora bakṣasthaḷa
<P>gajaripu jiṇiṇa tohora kaḷebara | 49 |
<P>gabhīra nābhi bitramasiṃgha ṭhāṇi majhāgoṭi
<P>haṃsulī tuḷiprāẏa śobhābana tora piṭhi | 50 |
<P>ḍāhāṇabrateka śaṃkhaprāẏe kaṇṭha śobhābana
<P>kheḷantā siṃgha jāṇi jagujana mohana | 51 |
<P>ulaṭa kadaḷī jāṇi tohora benijānu
<P>muhiṃ tohora apāda gheniyāi re abhimanu | 52 |

<P>pañchadīrgha sapata ārakta śobhani
<P>tinigabhīra khūrpa bistāra tini tini | 55 |
<P>chaḍasthāne ucca sūkṣuma pañchusthāna
<P>bābure tora batiśa guṇa lakṣaṇa | 56 |
<P>lakṣe lakṣaṇa gheni upujilu re mohora bābu
<P>daẏāsāgara databya śatesiṃgha prākarma sabu | 57 |
<P>ẏete lakṣaṇa gheni upujilu re dulāḷa
<P>ẏebeḷe mohora toṭi kāṭilu chāṇḍāḷa | 58 |
<P>bābu bāḷuta baẏasare tote pāḷibāku hoili
<P>bīrabara pratagyāṃ re tohora dekhira nuārili | 59 |
<P>robai pāṃlaguni ye keśabāsa asambhāḷa
<P>bhīmasena mukha chahiṃ pātha bolai bikaḷa | 60 |
<P>bīrabara brikodara pratagyaṃ nāma tuye bahi

<P>āre bābu nakuḷa abhimanu ye tohora gaḷāra kaṇṭhi

<P>bābu sahadeba re tu ta bhūtabhabiṣya jāṇu
<P>abhimanyura maraṇa kenhe tadanta na bakhāṇu | 64 |
<P>sugyāna kari yebe kahantu mora āge

<P>kebaṇa droha abhimanyu kalakire tote

<P>niropi chahiṃlā ye pāṭha yujheṣṭhidebaṃkara mukha
<P>niceṣṭa hoiṇa ye paḍila bibakṣa | 68 |
[MBO-08-137]
<P>koḷakari dhaile dharmarāẏa yujheṣṭhi
<P>robai sarbasācī mr̥ddhana yāuacchi phāṭi | 69 |

<P>mattagarba bhābe na cetanti puruṣa

<P1>mahāśokabhara hoiachaiṭi arajuna
<P1>putrara chaḷe na puṇa rātre karaiṭi sāṃgrāma |
<P1>nibāri nuāriba daibara kala kr̥tya
<P1>dr̥ṛha kari rātre jagathibaṭi bīra pātha |
<P1>āmbhe yāuachuṃ ye dwārikā bhmabana
<P1>rātra na pāhuṃ āsi miḷibu bahana |
<P1>samastaṃku prabodhanā kariṇa ruṣikeśī
<P1>ubha hoile swāmī bāhāra pure āsi |
<P1>nandighoṣa rathe dei chariaśwa yoci
<P1>dāruka sātukīki duāre rahāi śirībacchi |
<P1>āho arjuna dukhita hoicchi mahātrodhe
<P1>na puṇa rātre ẏekā uṭhiṇa yāi raṇa madhye |
<P1>bāhāra hoile āmbha rāṇa pakāi basāiba nei rathe
<P1>dhīra dhīra kari ratha bāhuthiba rātra pahibā pariyante
<P1>beḷa ghaḍike prabeśa hoibaṭi bhūadwāre
<P1>mohora aile paśiba samare |
<P1>bhīmasena nakuḷa ye sahadeba bhāi tini
<P1>dujadwāre rahile nijabaḷa gheni |
<P1>bainetra piṭhire bijaẏe jagabhūta
<P1>bijaẏe jagamohana dwārikā bhmabanantā |
<P1>rukmiṇī ye jāmbabatī kāḷandī satyabhāmā
<P1>arghya dei praḷamba hoile charibāmā |
<P1>swāmī apāra biḷamba ta kala āja rāti
<P1>1 jāḷandhara bhūara bāratā kahile śirīpati | [abaśiṣṭāṃśa para pr̥ṣṭhāre]
[MBO-08-173]
<P>badaẏanti agasti śuṇa baibasuta manu
<P>catrabhūa samare yahuṃ paḍilā abhimanyu | 4 |
<P1>[pūrba pr̥ṣṭhāra paṭhāntara]
<P1>arjunaku gheni āmbhe galu jāḷandhara bhūa raṇe
<P1>catrabhūa kapaṭa ẏeṇe kaleguru droṇe |
<P1>daśasahasra rājā māilā subhadrāra tanu
<P1>kapaṭa yuddhakari beḍhi māile abhimanyu |
<P1>apāra guṇa tāhāra kahile catrapāṇi
<P1>śuṇi śokakale satyabhāmā jāmbobatī rukmiṇī |
<P1>gobindeboile tumbhe najāṇa rukmiṇī śatrābatī
<P1>kāli jīiṃthile abhimanyu mārantā hari arjuna āmbha duhinti |
<P1>ẏesaneka acchinā ākāśara pūrbabāṇī
<P1>purandara ye swargaku nelā tāhā jāṇi |
<P1>swāmīku apacaẏa śuṇiṇa sarbasatī
<P1>chāḍileka trodha hoileka sarbe śānti |
<P1>samasta br̥ttānta kahile debarāẏe
<P1>aruṇa prakāśa pūrbadige hoẏe |
<P1>daibakī yaśodā ye abhimanyura hata śuṇi
<P1>karanti trodhe rodana uccasware bāṇī |
<P1>robanti mahādebī ye śire kara tāḍi
<P1>subhadrāra putrakaṣṭa abhimanyu guṇa sumari | [abaśiṣṭāṃśa para pr̥ṣṭhāre]
<P1>172 pr̥ṣṭhā 1--``jāḷandhara bhūara bāratā kahile śirīpati''--ẏehi pādapare
<>``cha'' pothire bhinma pāṭha :--

<P1>sakaḷa amuragaṇa samare pātha chedi |
<P1>catrabhūa kapaṭe rañchile droṇa guru
<P1>abhimanyu senāpati hoile hantakāru |
<P1>nabadwāra jiṇi galā mubhadrāra tanu
<P1>kapaṭe beḍhi māile kumāra abhimanyu |
<P1>apāra śokadhuni pāṇḍaba pañchabīre
<P1>kontī dropatī subhadrā loṭanti bhūiṃre |
<P1>ẏehānta prabodha karuṃ uchura raẏaṇī
<P1>abhimanyu hata śuṇi śokakale śrīkaṣṇa pāṭarāṇī |
[MBO-08-174]
<P>durāpada pratagyāṃ yahuṃ kalāka phālaguni

<P1>[pūrba pr̥ṣṭhāra pāṭhāntara]

<P1>dibya abalokanī kuṃkumabarṇṇa kāẏe |

<P1>tu mātā na chaḍa go maẏeṃṣāsura dānabaku |
<P1>1-ẏehāra badha nimante debatāẏe tote kale jāẏe
<P1>apādakhaṇḍanī go khaṇḍa apacaẏe |
<P1>maṃgaḷā boila maẏeṃṣā tapakalā ye pitāṃku
<P1>durapada bara dhātā dilāka ẏehāku |
<P1>biṣṇure bhaẏa boli maẏeṃṣā jāṇai ādikāḷe
<P1>puruṣe badha nohibi boilā sebeḷe |
<P1>yebaṇa stirīra hāthare maribi
<P1>jānu stana bhagamukha samasta dekhibi |
<P1>ẏesaneka bara pitāṃku magiacchi pūrbe
<P1>tu go mahāmāẏā ulagnaśāhī hoilbunā ẏebe |
<P1>ẏesaneka buddhi yahuṃ kahile debī sarbamaṃgaḷe
<P1>bibasana hoile debī maẏeṃṣara badhakāḷe |
<P1>chāmaṇḍā rūpare debī brahmāṇḍakhaṇḍa ghoṭi
<P1>2-durgāṃka rūpaku ye traẏalokye na ghaṭi |
<P1>thana jānu durgāṃkara ulagna ye śāhī
<P1>mohe baśa maẏeṃṣā durgāra jānu yaubana chahiṃ |
<P1>bhaga dekhi sānanda hoilā mahātamā
<P1>boilā debīra bhage yāi biśrāmu mora pañchu ātmā | [abaśiṣṭāṃśa para pr̥ṣṭhāre]
<P1>1-jāẏe--janma |
<P1>2-mahā biśr̥rūpe byāpile nabasr̥ṣṭi |(ga, na, ṭha, jha)
[MBO-08-182]
<P>baḍāi pratagyāṃ hāde kalāka phālaguni
<P>boilā jadyarathaku na māile kāli paśibi bahani | 13 |
<P1>[169 pr̥ṣṭhāra 124|2 ra pāṭhāntara]
<P1>trailokya aśakya yeuṃ bhagamārga
<P1>muṃ tāha dekhili ye ẏehi mohora bhāgya |
<P1>durgāra bhaga dekhi moheṇa baśa galā
<P1>pañchu bhūta ātmā ye maẏeṃṣā chaḍilā |
<P1>śūḷeṇa māḍi basile debī narāẏaṇī rūpe
<P1>debatāṃka uparaku dhāiṃle chāmaṇḍā rūpe kope |
<P1>ẏemante kari asuranta debataẏe dianti bara
<P1>bhakṣibi debatānta ye na thoibi swargapura |
<P1>mahā bhaẏāṃkāra dusaha nirāśa rūpa dekhi
<P1>1-paḷāile debatāẏe āsana upekṣi |
<P1>2-digāmbara puruṣe se paḷāile ḍare
<P1>3-samaste gopya hoile sāhera bhitare |
<P1>paḷābante īśwara ye hoile ulagnaśāhī
<P1>paḷāi nuāriṇa nr̥tyakaranti rahi |
<P1>lāṃgaṭa bhr̥ṃgaṭa hoi hari karanti nr̥tya
<P1>dekhi bhoḷa hoile durgā jagatamāta |
<P1>durgā boile iṣṭadebata sumara
<P1>ẏehikṣaṇi māri tote karibi āhāra |
<P1>īśware boile tuhi se pitāmātā
<P1>tohore śaraṇa muhiṃ tuhi se iṣṭadebatā | [abaśiṣṭāṃśa para pr̥ṣṭhāre]
<P1>1-paḷāiḷe debatāẏe gagana upekṣi |(cha, dha)
<P1>2-digāmbara sarūpe hara paḷāile ḍare |(bahupāṭha)
<P1>3-biśwambhara rūpa dekhi paḷāile bhaẏe
<>sabhiẏeṃ jaḷaśāhī tetiśakoṭi debatāẏe |(ca)
[MBO-08-183]
<P>[169 pr̥ṣṭhāra 124|2 ra pāṭhāntara]
<P1>āpada khaṇḍaṇī go jagatamāta tuhi
<P1>māra ki tāra go to tahuṃ āna nāhiṃ |
<P1>kārpuṇya bacana śuṇi toṣa jagatamāẏe
<P1>manāile bikaḷe khaṇḍilu apacaẏe |
<P1>bara māga jaṭiāre hoili tote śānti

<P>bharadwādaśaṃkara nandana ye kaicchā jagajjeṭhī

<P1>[169 pr̥ṣṭhāra 124|2 pāṭhāntara]
<P1>durgā ye bodhagale tohora satya bole
<P1>namaste kāntānī māgo sarbamaṅgaḷe |
<P1>jaẏatu durgā go jagata tāriṇī
<P1>saṃsāra āpāda khaṇḍu tu kariṇa bhramaṇi |

<P>śrīkr̥ṣṇa praśaṃsanti yoddhāṃkara dr̥ṛha āsana dekhi
<P>bihaḍanti aśwe aśuāra na upekṣi | 53 |
<P>keśaba pachāranti śuṇa ho dhanurjaẏa
<P>dui dui khaṇḍa hoiṇa rahichanti sabuṃkari kaẏe | 54 |
<P>katurī nārāja ye binddhalā sarbasācī
<P>samasta aśwaṃkara śiracchiḍi paḍuacchi | 55 |
<P>puṇa arjuna binddhale kāmyeka nāme śara
<P>surajita, bīrajita benirāẏe paḍile bhūmira | 56 |
<P>kaṭākṣa naẏane chāhiṃ adhare danta chāpi
<P>raṇaraṃga maṇḍaḷe paḍile sarbe byāpi | 57 |
<P>pāñchamarbhmata yoddhā pāñchamarbhmata aśwa
<P>beṛhi yuddha karuthile hoile bināśa | 58 |
<P>ẏesaneka prakāre arjunara mahimāṃ
<P>dekhiṇa āśrija ye hoile kr̥pabrahmā | 59 |
<P>yahuṃ raṇe bhaṃga hoileka sākhā
<P>pādānti sanyabaḷasamaste hoile nirekhā | 60 |
<P>ādrābaḷī sama dhanu dhariṇa kr̥pa āchāryye
<P>catrābrateka kariṇa binddhale nārāje | 61 |
<P>koṭiẏe kiraṇa jāṇi teja parakāśi
<P>dibibhmabi mahī ulukāpāta diśi | 62 |
<P>ratha gaja aśwe na rahile śahasre teja kari
<P>kauroba sanyabaḷa paḷābanti apasari | 63 |
<P>yojane pariyante jana manyuṣya kehi nāhiṃ
<P>kr̥paṃkara ratha nandighoṣa ratha duheṃ chanti rahi | 64 |
<P>śrīkr̥ṣṇa praśaṃsanti sādhu sādhu mahātamā
<P>chatrīkuḷe dekhili tohora baḍāi mahimāṃ | 65 |
<P1>59--pañcha marbhmata yoddhāṃkara ẏekai sarūpa
<>dekhiṇa āśrija ye hoileka kr̥pa |(adhikāṃśa pothi)
[MBO-08-212]
<P>ẏekasare rahiacchi kr̥paṃkara ratha
<P>kr̥ṣṇa arjunaṃku nārāja bindhai sāmaratha | 66 |
<P>dhārmika bibeka mahata kuḷaśīḷa
<P>bahuta praśaṃsile debakīra bāḷa | 67 |
<P>kr̥paṃka salaghanā śuṇi arjuna baḍa caḷi
<P>bahuta praśaṃsā tumbhe kala he banamāḷa | 68 |
<P>gobinde boile tu ki agyāna dhanañchaẏe
<P>nandighoṣa ratha tora meru tulya prāẏe | 69 |
<P>mahākalpa bañchantā tohora haẏe chāri
<P>rathadhwaja upare tohora hanumanta achai ābori | 70 |
<P>dutīpinākī sama gāṇḍima tohora kare
<P>paśupatra nārāja pūriacchi tohroa troṇare | 71 |
<P>aśeṣakoṭi brahmāṇḍa gheni muṃ tohora rathare sārathi
<P>śaṃkhacatra gadā gheni mohora narakeśarī mūrati | 72 |
<P>ẏe rūpa dekhi mohora śaṃkanti bedabrahmā
<P>jāṇili bhāroimalla aṭanti kr̥pabrahmā | 73 |
<P>taḷaku na thilā uparaku ta nohiba
<P>sādhu sādhu mahimāṃ tora bolanti bāsudeba | 74 |
<P>āho caitana kr̥paṃkara salaghanā dekhi pātha mahākopī
<P>guṇaghr̥ṣṭa kariṇa kare nārāja gheni kṣepi | 75 |
<P>haẏa sārathiṃki ye pāñcha pāñcha śara
<P>daśabāṇa prahārilā se sārathi upara | 76 |
<P>ābara pāñcha nārāja ye rathakaiṃ yoci
<P>kr̥paṃku hāboḍā śareka binddhalā sarbasācī | 77 |
<P>śa(?) gaḍante aśwe hoile sarbacūnā
<P>sārathi benikhaṇḍa hoi bhedilā kr̥paṃkara sehnā | 78 |
<P1>(?)
<P1>77|1--ābara pāñcha nārāja rathakaiṃ prāñchi |(ca)
[MBO-08-213]
<P>ratha śatekhaṇḍa hoi paḍilāka bhāji
<P>bhūmigate kr̥pa āchāryye paḍile gaḷagāji | 79 |
<P>puṇa kr̥tāntaka bāṇa peṣante arajuna
<P>raha raha pātha boli badaẏanti janārddana | 80 |
<P>mahāmantrabadī ẏe uttama brāhmaṇa
<P>badha karibā ẏehāku kebaṇa kāraṇa | 81 |
<P>biśeṣe paramaguru dorṇaṃkara śaḷā
<P>abaraṇa yoddhāẏe aśastamāṃkara mauḷā | 82 |
<P>kr̥pe bhūmigata upareṇa kr̥ṣṇa gale ratha bāhi
<P>beni odhi bhedi bije bhūa madhye yāiṃ | 83 |
<P>pāñchalakṣa yoddhā gheni rāẏeguru śalya
<P>nandighoṣa ogāḷile se bhāratakuḷa mahāmalla | 84 |

<P>parbate halanti ye bānara bighāte | 86 |
<P>aśi sahasra rathī tini marbhmata hāthī

<P>arddheka prabeśa ye hoiacchi dina
<P>andhāra ghoramaẏe diśai gagana | 89 |

<>ratha gaja diśanti tesane gahaḷa || (kha)

<P>ẏekaku āreka ye na kahanti uttara
<P>asaṃkṣepa kāḷe yenhe kampanti mahīdhara | 91 |
<P>sanya dekhi sānanda bīra phālaguni
<P>kopeṇa śara gheni binddhalāka tini | 92 |
<P>jaḷada medura pallaba tinibāṇa
<P>paḍante br̥ṣṭikalā dhārā ye śrābaṇa | 93 |
<P>andhāra ghora śareka māilā śākalya deśara rāẏe

<P>ohobaḷa thāṭhayāka hoile ye baṇā

<P>nandighoṣa beṛha caukati śara paḍuacchi
<P>ratha sārathi haẏe ye na diśai kicchi | 103 |
<P>śrībhmaje paraśu gheniṇa deba jagannāthe
<P>aneka nārāja ye chedile turite | 104 |

<P>samara sambhare pāiṇa mahādukha
<P>raṇa chaḍi paḷāi loḍanti pāiṇa bimukha | 115 |
<P>mana dr̥ṛhe yoddhāẏe bolanti raha raha re bābā

<P>sañjaẏe śakuni dhr̥tirāṣṭiṃkara tule
<P>daśa sahasra rathī gheni sindhurājā bāhāra hoile | 75 |
<P>aneka sambhare ye sindhu ādhipati
<P>gobinde dekhile jadyarathara mūrati | 76 |
<P1>74|1--kṣaṇe mātra chahiṃthāu arjunara mukha |(kha, ca)
<P1>76|2--``gobinde dekhile jadyarathara mūrati'' sthānare ``kha, na, tha''re adhikā pāṭha :--
<P1>aneka sānanda ye sindhurājā suta
<P1>kaurabaṃka saṃge ubhā hoi ānandita |
<P1>tatakṣaṇe arjuna ye dibyabeśa hoi
<P1>śrīphaḷa goṭiẏe nija kare ghenichaiṃ |
<P1>agnire paśiba boli bāsabara śiṣa
<P1>baiśwānara pāśe āsi hoilā prabeśa
<P1>lakṣeka mukutā kare gheni se prabeśa |
<P1>śrīkare śrīphaḷa gheni pātha bule bahni
<P1>paśibāku dr̥ṛhabrata kalā phālaguni |
[MBO-08-283]
<P>jadyaratha boilā ho śuṇa phālaguni
<P>adabhmate maraṇa tu ye ailu kāhuṃ gheni | 77 |
<P>tohora bairi aṭanti dhr̥tirāṣṭara poẏe
<P>āmbhanta māriloḍu tu kebaṇa bharasaẏe | 78 |
<P>dharma chaḍiṇa ye adharmakaiṃ kalu āśā
<P>kāḷe bihantā puruṣe tumbhanta kaleka nirāśā | 79 |
<P>ketekāḷa bratiba boli ati utakarme
<P>kāḷe āṇi śāsti tote bihilāka yame | 80 |
<P>durjananta bhaẏekari sajjananta loḍa māri
<P>marare pāṇḍabe akāḷacatra paḍi | 81 |
<P>śakuni boilā kr̥ṣṇa parā sārathi rathe thāuṃ thāuṃ
<P>śakaṭa bhūa bhedi nuārila kimpe kehu | 82 |
<P>akha caka bāṭe yebe bhedant aprathame
<P>pāñchaghaḍira madhye jadyarathakaiṃ bheṭanta sāṃgrāme | 83 |
<P>āpeṇe na jāṇilu nuārilu bhūa bhedi
<P>naśanta kāḷaku tumbhara biparīta buddhi | 84 |
<P>śakuni boilā pratagyāṃ kalu ati utakarmapaṇe
<P>dibārātra boli kiṃpe na boilu raṇe | 85 |
<P>ādyahuṃ jadyaratha tumbhanta aṭai urasala
<P>ẏehāra beḷe tumbhanta nohilā kicchi bhala | 86 |
<P>bhīmasena boilā tu śahasra gheni pātha
<P>ohosandhyāẏe nicaẏe māribā jadyaratha | 87 |

<P>dharma laghiṃṇa kathā ruhāibā ki pr̥thibi | 89 |

<P1>85|2--dibārātre boli kiṃpe na boilu baẏāṇe |(ṅa, tha)
[MBO-08-284]
<P>dinakara madhye pāranti yebe māri
<P>raṇe jaẏe sādhu sādhu huanā mohori | 90 |
<P>āu kṣaṇe yebe āditya debatā thānte rahi

<P>arjunara pratagyāṃ śuṇiṇa nārāẏaṇa

[MBO-08-285]
<P>gobinde boile tuho śahasra dhara pātha
<P>daśa śahasra yoddhā tule rahiachai jadyaratha | 100 |
<P>mānagobinda boilā ẏe kapaṭa kūṭa kathā
<P>dharmaku laghiṃbāra tumbhara hoilā sarbathā | 101 |
<P>chāriyuge sata dharmahiṃ se parichāra

<P>chāriśaṃkha bārāsa nabakṣauṇī pādānti | 82 |
<P>ẏeteka sanya gheniṇa aḷambuṣa rākṣasa

<P>benipadma aśwa yoddhā dile aḷāẏudhara mūḷe
<P>tu samara karibu ho ghaṭukāra tule | 84 |

<P>gobinde boile ho ki buddhi karibā pātha

<P>śalyaṃkara bacane se karṇṇa mahārathī
<P>dhyāẏe kari inda debatāṃku māgila bajra ye śakati | 65 |
<P>āsana kampanteṇa jāṇile maghabā

<P1>69|2--``muhiṃta na jāṇai śakati māgai ẏebe'' ehi pāṭha pare ``ṭa, ḍa, ta, tha'' re bhinma pāṭha --
<P1>indra boilā amare nirbātakapaca badha kalā arjuna
<P1>satya karāi boilā kapaca kuṇḍaḷa āṇi debu maghabāna |
<P1>arjunara bacane muṃ karṇṇara tahiṃki gali
<P1>kapaca kuṇḍaḷa bajra chauṃri tinihinti māgili |
<P1>dānabhārā pāi ratha na galā śūnyagati
<P1>leuṭi pratigraha deli bajra ye śakati |
<P1>br̥haspatiṃki bujhāi indra chaḍile bajra ye śakati
<P1>karṇṇaku prāpata hua āgyāṃ dile surapati |
<P1>bajra āsanteṇa phiṭilā raẏaṇī
<P1>śrīkare karṇṇa dhailā kṣatriẏa cūḍāmaṇi |

[MBO-08-424]

<P>tāhāra nandana ye aṭai puṣyadanta hāthī

[MBO-08-427]

<P1>495|2--se tīrthe snāna kalā sakaḷa pāpa galā tuṭi |(ja)
[MBO-08-434]
<P>aśwatthāmāra brahma astra praẏega,
<>droṇaṅkara mr̥ta piṇḍa dāha o aśwatthāmāra
<>śoka, astra śastra dāna
<P>badaẏanti agasti śuṇa baibasuta manu
<P>ratha tejyā kari āsuacchi droṇaṃkara tanu | 1 |
<P>yamunā nadī pāra hoi āsuchanti aśastamā
<P>trodhabhara hoiṇa yāuchanti kr̥pabrahmā | 2 |
<P>aśastamāku dekhile yamunā nadī kūḷe
<P>robanti kr̥pe ye bhiṇoiba bikeḷe | 3 |
<P>kr̥pe boile kāhiṃ thilu tu aśastamā
<P>tohora badha śuṇi droṇe hoile gata ātmā | 4 |
<P>aśastamāhata boli śubhilā yahūṃ bāṇī
<P>droṇe mr̥kṣāgata hoile putra hata śuṇi | 5 |
<P>dr̥padaṃka nandana dhr̥ṣṭa ye dyumana
<P>droṇamkara śira se chedilā bahana | 6 |
<P>droṇaṃka nāśa bāratā kahile yahuṃ kr̥pa
<P>śuṇi bhīṣma rūpa hoi aśastamā kalāka mahākopa | 7 |
<P>rāgeṇa aśastamā ye brahma astra dhari
<P>pāṇṭabanta māra boli śahasraku tiāri | 8 |
<P>dhr̥ṣṭadyumanaku pakāa begeṃ hāṇi
<P>mahā brahmā śahasra ye peṣile bege droṇi | 9 |
<P>ākāśa ghoṭiṇa ye āsai brahmaśara
<P>pāṇḍabanta ghoṭilā se beḷa benidaṇḍa bhitara | 10 |
<P>swarga mañcha bhmabana ulukāpāta prāẏe
<P>ohobaḷa saini paḷāile mahābhaẏe | 11 |
[MBO-08-435]
<P>sahadebakaiṃ pachārile deba ye śrībatsi
<P>apāra cahaḷa ta thāṭhare śubhmaacchi | 12 |
<P>sahadeba bolai śuṇimā nandabatsi
<P>aneka dhūruṃ deba aśastamā āsuacchi | 13 |
<P>bāṭare kahile tāṃku kr̥pa ye āchāryye
<P>śuṇikari kopa kale droṇaṃka ātnaje | 14 |
<P>swāmī ẏe ye brahmaśara aśastamā peṣi
<P>ẏehikṣaṇi samasta nāśiba ẏe ruṣikeśi | 15 |
<P>arjunakaiṃ chāhiṃ āgyāṃ dileka śrībatsa

<P>brahma śahasraku nārāẏaṇā śahasra sandhi

<P>ākāśe rahi nuārile br̥ndārake
<P>brahmāra bhubane yāiṃ kahile debaloke | 21 |
<P>nārāẏaṇa śasra brahma śara duhiṃkari teja ghāẏe
<P>samara chaḍi paḷāile kuru pāṇḍaba benirāẏe | 22 |
<P>driyodhana apasari hastinā pura yāiṃ
<P>pāṇṭaba baḷa yāi indrapraśastare sambhāi | 23 |
<P>ẏekā mātra samara bhūiṃre rahile kr̥ṣṇa pāṃlaguni
<P>kr̥pa aśastamāẏe rahile śasra gheni | 24 |
<P>caubiṃśa yojana ghuñchile beni baḷa

[MBO-08-436]
<P>mune muna paḍi tāḷa huante beni astre
<P>pr̥thī dala dalita hoilā kaṃpile giri parabate | 26 |

[MBO-08-437]
<P>āho mānagobinda tohora parā puruṣaku āmbhe āśrekalu
<P>kaḷapa taru taḷe thāi nirāṇa hoilu | 40 |
<P>pitā kāryya kari tora māna uddharai
<P>pañchu pāṇḍaba dhr̥ṣṭadyumana kr̥ṣṇa ādi muṃ mārai | 41 |

<P>samaraku bairāga se samasta śahasranta parityāgi
